      * Remove a key/value pair from the query string section of a URL
      */
     var removeURLParameter = function(url, parameter) {
       return url
         .replace(new RegExp('[?&]' + parameter + '=[^&#]*(#.*)?$'), '$1')
         .replace(new RegExp('([?&])' + parameter + '=[^&]*&'), '$1');
     };
 
     
             ga('create', 'UA-42508512-1', {"name":"dodo","cookieDomain":".thedodo.com"});
 
         
     
     // demographic reports
     ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
 
     ga('require', 'linkid', 'linkid.js');
 
         
   ga('dodo.set', {"dimension20":"_","dimension2":"homepage","dimension9":"editorial","dimension21":"","dimension23":"editorial"});
 
 
 
 
                     // Add Content Groups
                         ga('dodo.set', 'contentGroup1', 'homepage');
     
             var _canonicalUrl = 'https://www.thedodo.com/';
 
             // Remove query string if it exists
             if (_canonicalUrl.indexOf("?") > 0) {
                 _canonicalUrl = _canonicalUrl.substring(0, _canonicalUrl.indexOf("?"));
             }
 
             var queryString = removeURLParameter(window.location.search, 'pinn_uid');
 
             //Set the page to be the relative URL
             ga('dodo.set', 'page', _canonicalUrl.replace(/^.*\/\/[^\/]+/, '') + queryString);
 
             //Set the location to be the canonical URL
             ga('dodo.set', 'location', _canonicalUrl + queryString);
 
             //Anonymize IP Settings
             ga('dodo.set', 'anonymizeIp', true);
 
             //Track pageview
             ga('dodo.send', 'pageview');
 
             // Enhanced Ecommerce
             ga('dodo.require', 'ec');
             })();
   </script>
